Let r be (0 + -3)/(459/(-18)). Let x = 2526 + -15191/6. Let w = 11/2 + x. What is the closest to w in -3/2, r, -3?
r
Let v = 1 + 0. Let k = 0.1 - 1.1. Let q be (-3)/(-6)*2*3. Which is the closest to k?  (a) v  (b) 3/8  (c) q
b
Let m be (-5)/4 - 2/(-2). What is the nearest to -0.3 in -3, m, -0.5?
m
